<h6 class="kt-adv-heading16806_579d0b-77 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading16806_579d0b-77">Welcome To Parent Portfolio</h6>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading16806_d1e6f6-f8 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading16806_d1e6f6-f8">Meet Jacqueline &amp; Jonathan</h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center">As parents, we all want to give our children a great head start. We can accomplish this goal by investing financially in their future and investing our time with them to achieve their full potential.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Kids grow up in a blink of an eye. And, we understand time is precious. That’s why we firmly believe in building wealth and passive income to give us more time together.</p>
